</owl:Class>

</owl:Class>

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Play Record</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

[25/31] CQ57: How many players who have already spent money, spend money again?
======================================================================
<?xml version="1.0"?>

         xmlns:owl="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Player">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A person who participates in the game.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Game">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A specific game that can be played by players.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Achievement">

[30/31] CQ66: Where do the players who have done the most IAP live?

<?xml version="1.0"?>
<rdf:RDF xml:base="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#"
         xmlns:owl="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
         xmlns:rdf="http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#"
         xmlns:rdfs="http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#"
         xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#">

  <owl:Ontology rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#"/>

  <!-- owl:Class declarations -->

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Player">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A person who participates in the game.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Game">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A specific game that can be played by players.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Achievement">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A reward or milestone earned by a player in a game.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GamePlayRecord">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A record of a player's activity in a specific game, used to track metrics like time played.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Play Record</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AchievementType">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A category or classification of achievements, such as Combat, Exploration, or Story.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement Type</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Genre">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A category of games characterized by similar gameplay and themes.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Genre</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GameItem">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">An object or item that exists within the world of a game, such as a weapon, tool, or consumable.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Item</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Ability">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A specific power, effect, or capability associated with a game item.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Ability</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#PlayerGameInventory">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A pivot class representing the possession of a specific item by a player within a specific game.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player Game Inventory</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#InAppPurchase">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A record of a financial transaction made by a player to acquire items or services within a game.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">In-App Purchase</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Location">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A geographical place where a player resides, such as a city or country.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Location</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#PurchaseGameplayContext">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A pivot class linking an in-app purchase to the gameplay metrics (like hours played) at the time of purchase.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Purchase Gameplay Context</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Game">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A specific game that can be played by players.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Achievement">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GamePlayRecord">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Play Record</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AchievementType">

</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Genre">

</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GameItem">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Item</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Ability">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A specific power, effect, or capability associated with a game item.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Ability</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#PlayerGameInventory">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A pivot class representing the possession of a specific item by a player within a specific game.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player Game Inventory</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#InAppPurchase">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">In-App Purchase</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Location">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Location</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#PurchaseGameplayContext">

</owl:Class>
